  <a id="3303" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="3305" href="foundation.type-arithmetic-empty-type.html#7698" class="Function">map-right-unit-law-coprod-is-empty</a><a id="3339" class="Symbol">)</a>

    <a id="4134" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#4966" class="Function">is-not-contractible-Fin</a><a id="4157" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="4159" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#7403" class="Function">succ-Fin</a><a id="4167" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="4169" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#4856" class="Function">is-contr-Fin-one-ℕ</a><a id="4187" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
## Idea

2-element types are types that are merely equivalent to the standard 2-element type `Fin 2`.

## Definition

### The condition that a type has two elements

<pre class="Agda"><a id="has-two-elements-Prop"></a><a id="4368" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4368" class="Function">has-two-elements-Prop</a> <a id="4390" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4392" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4393" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4393" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="4395" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4397" href="Agda.Primitive.html#597" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="4402" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4404" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4406" href="foundation-core.universe-levels.html#235" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="4409" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4393" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="4411" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4413" href="foundation-core.propositions.html#1393" class="Function">UU-Prop</a> <a id="4421" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4393" class="Bound">l</a>
<a id="4423" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4368" class="Function">has-two-elements-Prop</a> <a id="4445" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4445" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="4447" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="4449" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types.html#4964" class="Function">has-cardinality-Prop</a> <a id="4470" class="Number">2</a> <a id="4472" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4445" class="Bound">X</a>

<a id="has-two-elements"></a><a id="4475" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4475" class="Function">has-two-elements</a> <a id="4492" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4494" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4495" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4495" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="4497" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4499" href="Agda.Primitive.html#597" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="4504" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4506" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4508" href="foundation-core.universe-levels.html#235" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="4511" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4495" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="4513" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4515" href="foundation-core.universe-levels.html#235" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="4518" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4495" class="Bound">l</a>
<a id="4520" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4475" class="Function">has-two-elements</a> <a id="4537" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4537" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="4539" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="4541" href="foundation-core.propositions.html#1495" class="Function">type-Prop</a> <a id="4551" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4552" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4368" class="Function">has-two-elements-Prop</a> <a id="4574" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4537" class="Bound">X</a><a id="4575" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="is-prop-has-two-elements"></a><a id="4578" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4578" class="Function">is-prop-has-two-elements</a> <a id="4603" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4605" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4606" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4606" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="4608" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4610" href="Agda.Primitive.html#597" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="4615" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4617" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4618" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4618" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="4620" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4622" href="foundation-core.universe-levels.html#235" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="4625" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4606" class="Bound">l</a><a id="4626" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4628" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4630" href="foundation-core.propositions.html#1309" class="Function">is-prop</a> <a id="4638" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4639" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4475" class="Function">has-two-elements</a> <a id="4656" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4618" class="Bound">X</a><a id="4657" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="4659" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4578" class="Function">is-prop-has-two-elements</a> <a id="4684" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4685" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4685" class="Bound">l</a><a id="4686" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4688" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4689" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4689" class="Bound">X</a><a id="4690" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4692" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="4694" href="foundation-core.propositions.html#1562" class="Function">is-prop-type-Prop</a> <a id="4712" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4713" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4368" class="Function">has-two-elements-Prop</a> <a id="4735" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4689" class="Bound">X</a><a id="4736" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
### The type of all 2-element types of universe level `l`

<pre class="Agda"><a id="2-Element-Type"></a><a id="4810" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4810" class="Function">2-Element-Type</a> <a id="4825" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4827" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4828" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4828" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="4830" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4832" href="Agda.Primitive.html#597" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="4837" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4839" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4841" href="foundation-core.universe-levels.html#235" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="4844" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4845" href="Agda.Primitive.html#780" class="Primitive">lsuc</a> <a id="4850" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4828" class="Bound">l</a><a id="4851" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="4853" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4810" class="Function">2-Element-Type</a> <a id="4868" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4868" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="4870" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="4872" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types.html#5255" class="Function">UU-Fin-Level</a> <a id="4885" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4868" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="4887" class="Number">2</a>

<a id="type-2-Element-Type"></a><a id="4890" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4890" class="Function">type-2-Element-Type</a> <a id="4910" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4912" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4913" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4913" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="4915" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4917" href="Agda.Primitive.html#597" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="4922" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4924" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4926" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4810" class="Function">2-Element-Type</a> <a id="4941" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4913" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="4943" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4945" href="foundation-core.universe-levels.html#235" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="4948" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4913" class="Bound">l</a>
<a id="4950" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4890" class="Function">type-2-Element-Type</a> <a id="4970" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="4972" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#605" class="Field">pr1</a>

<a id="has-two-elements-type-2-Element-Type"></a><a id="4977" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4977" class="Function">has-two-elements-type-2-Element-Type</a> <a id="5014" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="5018" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5019" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5019" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="5021" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5023" href="Agda.Primitive.html#597" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="5028" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5030" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5031" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5031" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="5033" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5035" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4810" class="Function">2-Element-Type</a> <a id="5050" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5019" class="Bound">l</a><a id="5051" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5053" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5055" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4475" class="Function">has-two-elements</a> <a id="5072" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5073" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4890" class="Function">type-2-Element-Type</a> <a id="5093" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5031" class="Bound">X</a><a id="5094" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="5096" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4977" class="Function">has-two-elements-type-2-Element-Type</a> <a id="5133" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="5135" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#617" class="Field">pr2</a>

  <a id="5174" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5175" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5175" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="5177" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5179" href="Agda.Primitive.html#597" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="5184" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5186" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5187" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5187" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="5189" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5191" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4810" class="Function">2-Element-Type</a> <a id="5206" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5175" class="Bound">l</a><a id="5207" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5209" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5211" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types.html#4004" class="Function">is-finite</a> <a id="5221" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5222" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4890" class="Function">type-2-Element-Type</a> <a id="5242" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5187" class="Bound">X</a><a id="5243" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="5245" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5140" class="Function">is-finite-type-2-Element-Type</a> <a id="5275" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5275" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="5277" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="5281" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types.html#11882" class="Function">is-finite-has-cardinality</a> <a id="5307" class="Number">2</a> <a id="5309" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5310" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4977" class="Function">has-two-elements-type-2-Element-Type</a> <a id="5347" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5275" class="Bound">X</a><a id="5348" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="finite-type-2-Element-Type"></a><a id="5351" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5351" class="Function">finite-type-2-Element-Type</a> <a id="5378" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5380" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4810" class="Function">2-Element-Type</a> <a id="5395" href="Agda.Primitive.html#764" class="Primitive">lzero</a> <a id="5401" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5403" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types.html#4743" class="Function">𝔽</a>
<a id="5405" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#605" class="Field">pr1</a> <a id="5409" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5410" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5351" class="Function">finite-type-2-Element-Type</a> <a id="5437" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5437" class="Bound">X</a><a id="5438" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5440" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="5442" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4890" class="Function">type-2-Element-Type</a> <a id="5462" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5437" class="Bound">X</a>

</pre>
## Properties

### The condition of having two elements is closed under equivalences

<pre class="Agda"><a id="5632" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="5639" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5639" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="5643" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5644" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5644" class="Bound">l1</a> <a id="5647" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5647" class="Bound">l2</a> <a id="5650" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5652" href="Agda.Primitive.html#597" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="5657" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5659" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5660" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5660" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="5662" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5664" href="foundation-core.universe-levels.html#235" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="5667" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5644" class="Bound">l1</a><a id="5669" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5671" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5672" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5672" class="Bound">Y</a> <a id="5674" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5676" href="foundation-core.universe-levels.html#235" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="5679" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5647" class="Bound">l2</a><a id="5681" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="5685" class="Keyword">where</a>
  
  <a id="5696" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5696" class="Function">has-two-elements-equiv</a> <a id="5719" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5721" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5660" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="5723" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#1621" class="Function Operator">≃</a> <a id="5725" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5672" class="Bound">Y</a> <a id="5727" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5729" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4475" class="Function">has-two-elements</a> <a id="5746" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5660" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="5748" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5750" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4475" class="Function">has-two-elements</a> <a id="5767" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5672" class="Bound">Y</a>
  <a id="5771" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5696" class="Function">has-two-elements-equiv</a> <a id="5794" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5794" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="5796" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5796" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="5798" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="5800" href="foundation.mere-equivalences.html#2257" class="Function">transitive-mere-equiv</a> <a id="5822" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5796" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="5824" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5825" href="foundation.propositional-truncations.html#2132" class="Function">unit-trunc-Prop</a> <a id="5841" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5794" class="Bound">e</a><a id="5842" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="5847" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5847" class="Function">has-two-elements-equiv&#39;</a> <a id="5871" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5873" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5660" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="5875" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#1621" class="Function Operator">≃</a> <a id="5877" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5672" class="Bound">Y</a> <a id="5879" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5881" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4475" class="Function">has-two-elements</a> <a id="5898" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5672" class="Bound">Y</a> <a id="5900" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5902" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4475" class="Function">has-two-elements</a> <a id="5919" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5660" class="Bound">X</a>

#### If `X` is a 2-element type, then evaluating an equivalence `Fin 2 ≃ X` at `0` is an equivalence

<pre class="Agda"><a id="11042" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="11049" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#11049" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="11053" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="11054" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#11054" class="Bound">l1</a> <a id="11057" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11059" href="Agda.Primitive.html#597" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="11064" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="11066" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11067" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#11067" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="11069" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11071" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4810" class="Function">2-Element-Type</a> <a id="11086" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#11054" class="Bound">l1</a><a id="11088" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="11092" class="Keyword">where</a>

#### The type of pointed 2-element types of any universe level is contractible

<pre class="Agda"><a id="13807" class="Keyword">abstract</a>
  <a id="is-contr-total-UU-Fin-Level-two-ℕ"></a><a id="13818" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#13818" class="Function">is-contr-total-UU-Fin-Level-two-ℕ</a> <a id="13852" class="Symbol">:</a>
    <a id="13858" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13859" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#13859" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="13861" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13863" href="Agda.Primitive.html#597" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="13868" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="13870" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13872" href="foundation-core.contractible-types.html#1006" class="Function">is-contr</a> <a id="13881" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13882" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#515" class="Record">Σ</a> <a id="13884" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13885" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types.html#5255" class="Function">UU-Fin-Level</a> <a id="13898" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#13859" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="13900" class="Number">2</a><a id="13901" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13903" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13904" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types.html#5350" class="Function">type-UU-Fin-Level</a> <a id="13922" class="Number">2</a><a id="13923" class="Symbol">))</a>

    <a id="13972" href="foundation-core.contractible-types.html#3813" class="Function">is-contr-equiv&#39;</a>

### Any automorphism on `Fin 2` is an involution

</pre>
### The swapping equivalence has no fixpoints

### Evaluating an automorphism at `0 : Fin 2` is a group homomorphism

<pre class="Agda"><a id="preserves-add-aut-point-Fin-two-ℕ"></a><a id="28894" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#28894" class="Function">preserves-add-aut-point-Fin-two-ℕ</a> <a id="28928" class="Symbol">:</a>

  <a id="28990" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="28992" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#8826" class="Function">aut-point-Fin-two-ℕ</a> <a id="29012" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#28933" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="29014" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#7869" class="Function Operator">∘e</a> <a id="29017" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#8826" class="Function">aut-point-Fin-two-ℕ</a> <a id="29037" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#28935" class="Bound">b</a><a id="29038" class="Symbol">)</a>

### Any Σ-type over `Fin 2` is a coproduct

<pre class="Agda"><a id="is-coprod-Σ-Fin-two-ℕ"></a><a id="29510" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#29510" class="Function">is-coprod-Σ-Fin-two-ℕ</a> <a id="29532" class="Symbol">:</a>

### There can't be three distinct elements in a 2-element type
